15:         val bookingsJsonString = sharedPreferences.getString(KEY_BOOKINGS, null) ?: return emptyList()
16:         return try {
17:             val jsonArray = JSONArray(bookingsJsonString)
18:             val bookings = mutableListOf<Booking>()
19:             for (i in 0 until jsonArray.length()) {
20:                 bookings.add(Booking.fromJsonObject(jsonArray.getJSONObject(i)))
21:             }
22:             bookings.sortedByDescending { it.timestamp }
23:         } catch (e: Exception) {
24:             e.printStackTrace()
25:             emptyList()
26:         }
27:     }
28: 
29:     fun saveBooking(booking: Booking) {
30:         val bookings = getBookings().toMutableList()
31:         bookings.removeAll { it.id == booking.id }
32:         bookings.add(booking)
33:         saveAllBookings(bookings)
34:     }
35: 
36:     fun deleteBooking(bookingId: String) {
37:         val bookings = getBookings().toMutableList()
38:         bookings.removeAll { it.id == bookingId }
39:         saveAllBookings(bookings)
40:     }
41: 
42:     private fun saveAllBookings(bookings: List<Booking>) {
43:         val jsonArray = JSONArray()
44:         bookings.forEach { jsonArray.put(it.toJsonObject()) }
45:         sharedPreferences.edit().putString(KEY_BOOKINGS, jsonArray.toString()).apply()
46:     }
47: }
48: 
The above content shows the entire, complete file contents of the requested file.

I have created a detailed implementation plan for the new interactive 2D Grid View for adding bookings. 

You can find the plan here: [implementation_plan.md](file:///C:/Users/agraw/.gemini/antigravity-ide/brain/5a288740-4596-47dd-b37f-aee92aa85b80/implementation_plan.md).

### Highlight of the Design:
* **No Loss of Existing Form:** A beautiful sliding toggle at the top of the "Add Booking" tab will let you switch between **Form View** (the current design with all detailed fields and dorm features) and the new **Interactive Grid View**.
* **Smooth 2D Scrolling:** The leftmost date column and the topmost room header row will remain sticky, and all rows will scroll horizontally in perfect synchronization.
* **Curated Platform Colors:** Booking cells will be color-coded by booking platform (Indigo, Green, Blue, Purple) and payment status (Amber for pending) to look clean and premium in both Light and Dark themes.

Please review the plan and let me know if you approve so I can proceed with implementing it!

+@Composable
+fun getPlatformColors(platform: String, isPending: Boolean): Pair<Color, Color> {
+    val isDark = isSystemInDarkTheme()
+    return if (isDark) {
+        if (isPending) {
+            Pair(Color(0xFF5D4037), Color(0xFFFFCC80)) // Dark brown/orange, light orange text
+        } else {
+            when (platform) {
+                "Direct" -> Pair(Color(0xFF1A237E), Color(0xFFC5CAE9))      // Dark Indigo, light Indigo text
+                "MMT" -> Pair(Color(0xFF1B5E20), Color(0xFFC8E6C9))         // Dark Green
+                "Booking.com" -> Pair(Color(0xFF0D47A1), Color(0xFFBBDEFB)) // Dark Blue
+                "Agoda" -> Pair(Color(0xFF4A148C), Color(0xFFE1BEE7))       // Dark Purple
+                else -> Pair(Color(0xFF263238), Color(0xFFCFD8DC))          // Dark Grey
+            }
+        }
+    } else {
+        if (isPending) {
+            Pair(Color(0xFFFFF3E0), Color(0xFFE65100)) // Light orange, dark orange text
+        } else {
+            when (platform) {
+                "Direct" -> Pair(Color(0xFFE8EAF6), Color(0xFF1A237E))      // Light Indigo, dark Indigo text
+                "MMT" -> Pair(Color(0xFFE8F5E9), Color(0xFF1B5E20))         // Light Green
+                "Booking.com" -> Pair(Color(0xFFE3F2FD), Color(0xFF0D47A1)) // Light Blue
+                "Agoda" -> Pair(Color(0xFFF3E5F5), Color(0xFF4A148C))       // Light Purple
+                else -> Pair(Color(0xFFECEFF1), Color(0xFF263238))          // Light Grey
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}

+@Composable
+fun DetailRow(label: String, value: String) {
+    Row(
+        modifier = Modifier
+            .fillMaxWidth()
+            .padding(vertical = 2.dp),
+        horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.SpaceBetween,
+        verticalAlignment = Alignment.Top
+    ) {
+        Text(
+            text = label,
+            fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold,
+            fontSize = 12.sp,
+            color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurfaceVariant,
+            modifier = Modifier.weight(1f)
+        )
+        Text(
+            text = value,
+            fontSize = 13.sp,
+            color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurface,
+            modifier = Modifier.weight(1.5f),
+            textAlign = TextAlign.End
+        )
+    }
+}

### What you can test now on your phone:
1. **Multiple Bookings on Same Cell:** Adding multiple bookings to the same room on the same date will split the grid cell vertically and show both bookings (color-coded by platform).
2. **Cell Details Dialog:** Clicking any cell opens a dialog listing all bookings for that cell with a `+ Add Booking` button at the bottom.
3. **Palette Edit Flow:** Clicking on any booking card in the cell list opens the Quick Book/Edit dialog, allowing you to edit the booking details or delete it entirely.

### 🤖 Antigravity Assistant
Created At: 2026-06-15T02:58:55Z
Completed At: 2026-06-15T02:59:00Z
The search for "Failed to collect certificates from base.apk using APK Signature Scheme v2 SHA 256 digest of contents did not verify adb install" returned the following summary:
The error **`INSTALL_PARSE_FAILED_NO_CERTIFICATES: Failed to collect certificates ... using APK Signature Scheme v2: SHA-256 digest of contents did not verify`** generally indicates that the Android system cannot verify the integrity of the APK file you are trying to install[1][2][3].

This is often caused by a corrupt file, an issue with the signing process, or a hardware communication error[1][4]. Below are the most effective ways to resolve this:

### 1. Uninstall the Existing App First
If you have a different version of the same app already installed on your device (e.g., a release version vs. a debug version), the signatures will mismatch, causing this error[3][5][6].
*   **Action:** Manually uninstall the app from your device/emulator, then try the `adb install` command again[3][6].

### 2. Check Your Hardware (USB Cable)
This is a surprisingly common cause for "digest" errors[1]. If you are using a poor-quality USB cable, an adapter, or a faulty port, data corruption can occur during the transfer to the device[1].
*   **Action:** Try a high-quality, direct USB-C cable (no adapters or hubs) and switch to a different USB port on your computer[1].

### 3. Rebuild the Project
The build process might have failed to sign the APK correctly, or a previous build artifact may be interfering[1][7].
*   **Action:**
    *   Perform a "Clean Project" and "Rebuild Project" in Android Studio[1].
    *   Delete the `build` folders in your project directory manually and build again.

### 4. Verify Signing Configuration
If you are manually signing the APK or using specific build tools, ensure the V2 signing scheme is correctly applied[8].
*   **Action:** 
    *   When generating a signed APK in Android Studio, ensure the **"V2 (Full APK Signature)"** checkbox is selected in the "Sign

1: # Implementation Plan - Interactive Grid View for Add Booking
2: 
3: This plan outlines the design and changes to introduce an interactive 2D Grid View for the "Add Booking" tab, while keeping the existing form-based implementation intact and easily switchable.
4: 
5: ## User Review Required
6: 
7: > [!NOTE]
8: > We will add a beautiful, sliding tab selector at the top of the **Add Booking** tab to switch between **Form View** and **Interactive Grid View**. This ensures that the user doesn't lose the existing detailed booking form (including Dorm features), but can try out the new Grid View.
9: 
10: ## Proposed Changes
11: 
12: ### Android Application Layer
13: 
14: #### [MODIFY] [MainActivity.kt](file:///c:/HOC/app/app/src/main/java/com/sparsh/myapplication/MainActivity.kt)
15: - Pass the full list of `bookings` and the `onDeleteBooking` callback to the `AddBookingScreen` so that the grid can query bookings and perform deletions directly from cell popups.

st column displaying dates (e.g., "1 Mon", "2 Tue"..."31 Sun").

26:   - **Grid Cell Rendering**:
27:     - **Empty Cell**: Dotted borders with a subtle hover/click indicator. Clicking triggers a "Quick Book" Dialog.
28:     - **Booked Cell**: Curved card with harmonious color-coding (based on platform e.g., Direct: Indigo, MMT: Green, Booking.com: Blue, Agoda: Purple) and displaying the booked price (e.g., `₹3,200`). A pending payment status shows an orange/amber color. Clicking triggers a "Booking Details" Dialog.
29:   - **Dialogs**:
30:     - **Quick Book Dialog**: Form fields for Guest Name, Platform (dropdown), Rate/Price (pre-filled or custom), Payment Status (Paid/Pending), Payment Method (UPI/Cash/Card/Bank Transfer), Expenses, and Notes. Validates input and triggers `onAddBooking`.
31:     - **Booking Details Dialog**: Displays guest details, platform, rate, payment status, payment method, expenses, and notes, with options to **Delete** or dismiss.

196:                 "Agoda" -> Pair(Color(0xFF4A148C), Color(0xFFE1BEE7))       // Dark Purple
197:                 else -> Pair(Color(0xFF263238), Color(0xFFCFD8DC))          // Dark Grey
198:             }
199:         }

201:         if (isPending) {

185: @Composable
186: fun getPlatformColors(platform: String, isPending: Boolean): Pair<Color, Color> {
187:     val isDark = isSystemInDarkTheme()
188:     return if (isDark) {
189:         if (isPending) {
190:             Pair(Color(0xFF5D4037), Color(0xFFFFCC80)) // Dark brown/orange, light orange text
191:         } else {
192:             when (platform) {
193:                 "Direct" -> Pair(Color(0xFF1A237E), Color(0xFFC5CAE9))      // Dark Indigo, light Indigo text

602: @OptIn(ExperimentalMaterial3Api::class)
603: @Composable
604: fun QuickBookDialog(
605:     date: String,
606:     roomNumber: String,
607:     bookingToEdit: Booking? = null,
608:     isDormMode: Boolean = false,
609:     onDismiss: () -> Unit,
610:     onConfirm: (Booking) -> Unit,
611:     onDelete: ((String) -> Unit)? = null
612: ) {
613:     var guestName by remember { mutableStateOf("") }
614:     var platform by remember { mutableStateOf("Direct") }
615:     var isBillOn by remember { mutableStateOf(false) }
616:     var billAmountStr by remember { mutableStateOf("") }
617:     var expensesStr by remember { mutableStateOf("") }
618:     var paymentStatus by remember { mutableStateOf("Paid") }
619:     var paymentMethod by remember { mutableStateOf("UPI") }
620:     var notes by remember { mutableStateOf("") }
621: 
622:     var showError by remember { mutableStateOf(false) }
623:     var errorMessage by remember { mutableStateOf("") }
624: 
625:     var dialogRoomItems by remember { mutableStateOf(listOf<BookingItem>()) }
626:     var dialogItemRatesMap by remember { mutableStateOf(mapOf<String, String>()) }
627: 
628:     LaunchedEffect(bookingToEdit, roomNumber) {
629:         if (bookingToEdit != null) {
630:             guestName = bookingToEdit.guestName
631:             platform = bookingToEdit.platform

### 🤖 Antigravity Assistant
I have successfully implemented all requirements for cross-booking and divided pricing!

### Summary of What Was Done

1. **Option to Mix Rooms & Dorm Beds**:
   - Replaced the single add button inside the booking dialog with two side-by-side buttons: **`+ Add Room`** and **`+ Add Bed`**.
   - Added visual container tags (`Room` vs `Dorm`) next to each allocated item row to easily identify them.
   - Placeholders (`Room No` or `Bed No`) dynamically update based on the item's category.

2. **Divided Pricing Logic for Dorm Beds**:
   - Introduced a **`Total Dorm Price`** input field that dynamically renders whenever there is at least one `"Dorm"` bed item in the booking list.
   - For `"Room"` items, individual rate fields remain fully editable (individual pricing).
   - For `"Dorm"` items, individual rate fields are disabled and replaced by a text display showing **`₹X each`** (where `X` is `Total Dorm Price / number of dorm beds`). This recalculates instantly on re-composition as you modify the total price or add/remove beds.
   - On saving, the total dorm price is split equally among the dorm items.

3. **General Text Adjustments**:
   - Updated custom bill total descriptions and deletion warnings to dynamically handle mixed configurations.

4. **Testing and Verification**:
   - Kotlin compilation was verified successfully via Gradle.
   - Assembled and deployed the debug build to `emulator-5554`.
   - Verified the behavior interactively on the emulator by creating a mixed booking of `Room 101` and `Bed A1`, allocating a total dorm price, confirming it, and seeing the correct room pricing on the Rooms Grid and bed pricing on the Dorms Grid.
   - Updated [task.md](file:///C:/Users/agraw/.gemini/antigravity-ide/brain/5a288740-4596-47dd-b37f-aee92aa85b80/task.md) and [walkthrough.md](file:///C:/Users/agraw/.gemini/antigravity-ide/brain/5a288740-4596-47dd-b37f-aee92aa85b80/walkthrough.md) with details and emulator screenshots.
